<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman"><B>NOTE I &#150; Stockholders&#146; Equity</B></FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:47pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>Preferred Stock</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>&nbsp;</B>On August 12, 2015 the Company approved an increase of their preferred shares from 50,000,000 to 200,000,000.<B> </B>The Company is authorized to issue up to 200,000,000 shares of preferred stock, $0.0001 par value (&#147;Preferred Stock&#148;), which is convertible to common at .01 to 1. &nbsp;The Board of Directors authorized to fix the designations, rights, preferences, powers and limitations of each series of Preferred Stock. &nbsp;The Company&#146;s prior CEO, Clark Ortiz currently holds 25,000,000 shares of the Company&#146;s preferred stock.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On September 26, 2014 the Board of Directors authorized an amendment to the articles of incorporation to authorize 10,000,000 shares each preferred stock class B and class C. &nbsp;These shares have a $.0001 par value, have voting rights of 1,000 to 1 and are convertible to common at 1 to 1 and 10 to 1 respectively.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On August 12, 2015, the Company approved a reverse stock split of their common stock at 1,000 shares to 1. &nbsp;In conjunction with this reverse, the rate at which preferred stock is convertible to common was also impacted by the same 1,000 rate. The new conversion rates are reflected above.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:49.5pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:47.5pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>Common Stock&nbsp;</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:49.5pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On March 25, 2014 the Company amended their authorized Common Stock to 5,000,000,000 shares from 1,000,000,000 shares. </P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;On March 21, 2014 the Company resolved to adopt the 2014 Incentive Stock Option and Restricted Stock Plan. &nbsp;The purpose of this Plan is to provide a means by which eligible recipients may be given an opportunity to benefit from increases in value of the Common Stock through the granting of the following: (i) Incentive Stock Options, (ii) Nonqualified Stock Options, (iii) rights to acquire restricted stock, and (iv) stock appreciation rights. &nbsp;Eligible Award recipients are the employees, directors and consultants of the Company and its Affiliates. The Company also seeks to retain the services of the group of persons eligible to receive Awards, to secure and retain the services of new members of this group and to provide incentives for such persons to exert maximum efforts for the success of the Company and its Affiliates. &nbsp;450,000,000 shares of common stock are registered to this plan at an offering price of $0.001. &nbsp;The Plan shall expire on March 20, 2024.&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On August 12, 2015, the Company approved a reverse stock split of their common stock at 1,000 shares to 1.</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Common Stock&nbsp;</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On October 13, 2015, the Company resolved to adopt the Employees, Directors and Consultants Stock Plan for the Year 2015. &nbsp;The purpose of this Plan is to enable the Company, to promote the interests of the Company and its stockholders by attracting and retaining employees, directors and consultants capable of furthering the future success of the Company and by aligning their economic interests more closely with those of the Company&#146;s stockholders, by paying their fees or salaries in the form of shares of the Company&#146;s common stock. &nbsp;500,000,000 shares of common stock are registered to this plan at an offering price of $0.0001. &nbsp;The Plan shall expire on January 1, 2017.&nbsp;</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE J &#150; Commitments and Contingencies</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>Various creditors have brought legal proceedings for collections of their claims against the Company. &nbsp;Judgments payable at December 31, 2015 and 2014 are $1,138,264 and $1,102,510, respectively.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE K &#150; Related Party Transactions</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman; margin-bottom: -12pt;" align=justify>The Company has borrowed $1,100,611 from a former member of the Board of Directors and two (2) related parties. The related party notes total to $5,611. &nbsp;Two of the notes from the former Board of Directors total to $1,045,000 and are unsecured. &nbsp;The third note in the amount of $50,000 is secured by a second lien on the Company&#146;s assets. &nbsp;The notes to the former member of the Board of Directors are in default and the Company has included approximately $1,293,114 of accrued interest in accrued expenses at December 31, 2015.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman; margin-bottom: -12pt;" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>Payments of Company expenses have been made by current members of the board of directors in the amount of $4,255 through December 31, 2015 of which $2,174 is included in notes payable affiliates. &nbsp;Payments in the amount of $2,081 have been forgiven by the members and are included in additional paid in capital at December 31, 2015. </P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE L &#150; Fair Value</B>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>The Company has categorized its assets and liabilities recorded at fair value based upon the fair value hierarchy specified by GAAP.&nbsp; All assets and liabilities are recorded at historical cost which approximates fair value, and therefore, no items were valued according to these inputs.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>The levels of fair value hierarchy are as follows:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:49.5pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:79.2pt; text-indent:-19.8pt; font-family:Symbol" align=justify><FONT FACE="Symbol">&#183;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:79.2pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman">Level 1 inputs utilize unadjusted quoted prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that the Company has the ability to access;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
</P>
<P align="center" style="line-height:13pt; margin:0pt; font-size:11pt; align=center;page-break-before:always; margin-bottom: 0pt;">30</P>
<br>

<P style="margin:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P align="center" style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman"><B>SOOUM CORP.</B></P>
<P align="center" style="margin:0pt; font-family:new times roman"><FONT FACE="new times roman"><B>New York, New York</B></FONT></P>
<P align="center" style="margin:0pt; font-family:new times roman">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:45.35pt; padding-bottom:3pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:new times roman; border-bottom:2.25pt solid #000000" align=center><B>NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman"><B>NOTE L &#8211; &nbsp;Fair Value</B></FONT>&nbsp;<B>&#8211; continued</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:79.2pt; text-indent:-19.8pt; font-family:Symbol" align=justify><FONT FACE="Symbol">&#183;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:79.2pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman">Level 2 inputs utilize other-than-quoted prices that are observable, either directly or indirectly. &nbsp;Level 2 inputs include quoted prices for similar assets and liabilities in active markets, and inputs such as interest rates and yield curves that are observable at commonly quoted intervals; and</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:79.2pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:79.2pt; text-indent:-19.8pt; font-family:Symbol" align=justify><FONT FACE="Symbol">&#183;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:79.2pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman">Level 3 inputs are unobservable and are typically based on our own assumptions, including situations where there is little, if any, market activity.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>In certain cases, the inputs used to measure fair value may fall into different levels of the fair value hierarchy. &nbsp;In such cases, the Company categorizes such financial asset or liability based on the lowest level input that is significant to the fair value measurement in its entirety. &nbsp;Our assessment of the significance of a particular input to the fair value measurement in its entirety requires judgment and considers factors specific to the asset or liability.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>Both observable and unobservable inputs may be used to determine the fair value of positions that are classified within the Level&nbsp;3 category. &nbsp;All assets and liabilities are at cost which approximates fair value and there are not items that were required to be valued on a non-recurring basis.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:48.25pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>The following liabilities were valued at fair value as of December 31, 2015 and 2014. No other items were valued at fair value on a recurring or non-recurring basis as of December 31, 2015 and 2014.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=center><BR></P>

<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="times new roman"><B>NOTE M &#150; Merger</B></FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On September 23, 2014 the Company signed a merger agreement with SoOum Corp., a Delaware corporation. &nbsp;Per the agreement, the outstanding shares of SoOum Corp common stock will be converted into 6,768,955 shares of the Company&#146;s preferred stock. &nbsp;This transfer of stock will result in an eighty percent (80%) ownership interest of the Company. Upon completion, the Company will be the surviving corporation and SoOum will be a wholly owned subsidiary. At the date of merger, $480,000 goodwill was acquired and posted to the Company. &nbsp;At December 31, 2014 the goodwill amount of $480,000 was impaired (See Note N).</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE N &#150; Impairment of Goodwill</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>At December 31, 2014 the Company evaluated the balance of goodwill and determined that it had a value of $-0-. &nbsp;The Company therefore impaired goodwill in the amount of $480,000 at December 31, 2014.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE O &#150; Liability for Conversion Feature of Preferred Shares</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>Upon the issuance of the Series B Preferred and the Series C Preferred for the SoOum Corp acquisition, the owners of these securities were entitled to receive in total 80% of the common stock of the Company upon full conversion. &nbsp;Assuming full conversion at a fixed conversion ratio, based on the common shares outstanding at December 31, 2014, there would be 26,250,000,000 shares common that would be converted, which is 25,690,960,686 more shares than the current authorized amount. &nbsp;Based on the stock price at December 31, 2014, $.0005, the total value of those shares would be $12,845,480. &nbsp;In accordance with Generally Accepted Accounting Principles, the Company recorded a liability for that amount on the financial statements. During the year ended December 31, 2015, the liability was reduced to $-0- as the reversal of produced enough stock to avoid a conversion deficiency.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify><B>NOTE P &#150; Subsequent Events</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; text-indent:-45.35pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:44.6pt; font-family:times new roman" align=justify>On August 25, 2016 the Company entered into an exchange agreement with Western Grade, LLC. &nbsp;Under the terms of the exchange agreement, Western Grade members will exchange their ownership interest for 420,000,000 shares of the common stock of the Company, which represents 42% ownership in the Company. &nbsp;Western Grade will therefore be a wholly owned subsidiary of the Company.</P>
